 darasal east india railway cameti ke chairman sar wiliam ekworth ne 1924 main rail bajet ko aam bajet se alag karne kaa prastaav rakhaa
 In 1924, the share of the railway budget was 70 percent
 itani badi hissedari ko dekhakar hi ise aam bajet se alag karne ke prastaav ko sweekaar kar liya gaya
